Coming out of the post-Siege period he had cycled through three sequential institutional roles in rapid succession — leader of the underground Avengers in Civil War, leader of the post-occupation New Avengers, then leader of a reconstituted Mighty Avengers structured deliberately around street-level, non-Manhattan-elite operators (the team's roster choices — Power Man (Victor Alvarez), White Tiger, Blue Marvel, Spectrum, the Falcon — are documentary evidence of his preferences when given roster authority: working-class, predominantly Black and Brown, scientifically credible but not Stark-credentialed, mostly Harlem-and-Brooklyn-anchored). He then accepted Steve Rogers's request to head the reformed Thunderbolts. He resigned that role within months of operational onset over the program's compromises around lethal force and supervillain handlers' interference. The Thunderbolts arc is the cleanest single example of his characterological loop — accept the institutional ask out of respect for the asker, hold the line as long as the line is honorable, walk when it isn't, walk publicly. He does not sabotage on exit; he simply leaves and tells you why.

He then returned to the Heroes for Hire shingle as a private operation, and ran it as a working business with Misty Knight handling logistics. This is the period in which he was visibly happiest in the canon — married, father of a young daughter, partnered with Rand again intermittently, anchored to Harlem, beholden to no team flag. The file flags this period as his baseline equilibrium state — the condition to which all subsequent disruptions can be measured.

### 4.2 The Mortality Event (Cage, 2017)

The single most consequential medical event of the recent era was the contamination/relapse storyline in which a corrupted iteration of the Burstein process — administered by adversarial parties working from leaked or reverse-engineered notes — induced a degenerative cellular cascade. Operationally: his durability fluctuated; he experienced focal weakness; he registered, for the first time on the record, sustained pain that did not resolve quickly. Behaviorally he did what he always does — concealed the severity from the chosen unit until concealment was untenable, sought help from a Burstein-adjacent technical authority rather than a general medical facility, and treated the entire affair as an operational problem rather than a mortality problem in front of others.

This is diagnostic. The file emphasizes the gap between the affect he displayed (terse, joke-light, functional) and the affect implied by his behavioral micro-changes during the arc: increased time on the phone with his wife in non-tactical conversation; increased physical contact with the child (visible on the page as scenes of carrying Danielle when carrying her was not necessary); a marked decrease in solo patrol and a corresponding increase in domestic presence. He was, in the technical sense, putting affairs in order without admitting to himself that he was doing so. The mortality anxiety reactivated the Burstein-trauma signature — refusal of conventional medicine, hostility to needles, an irrational but durable resistance to any cure-narrative offered by a white-coated stranger. He survived the arc. The residue persisted.

### 4.3 The Mayoralty (Devil's Reign and after)

The single most ideologically dissonant period of his entire life followed shortly thereafter. In the wake of the Wilson Fisk mayoral catastrophe and the public collapse of trust in the office, the subject accepted the New York mayoralty. This decision should be read with appropriate weight: a man whose foundational operational code is *institutions lie until proven otherwise* and *rules that cannot survive contact with Harlem are not rules worth obeying* walked into the most institutional office available to a non-federal civilian in the United States.

The file infers the decision sequence from his behavior: (a) the office was offered in a moment of acute civic emergency in which refusal would have left it in worse hands; (b) Jessica Jones was consulted and did not veto, which under his current operational architecture is the closest thing he has to an authorizing body; (c) he calculated, correctly, that he could not credibly continue to demand that institutions earn his trust if he refused to demonstrate that the institution could be inhabited by someone like him without corruption; (d) the symbolic stakes — a Black ex-convict, framed and tortured by the carceral state, sworn in as mayor of the city that had failed him — were too historically resonant for him to refuse.

He served. He governed. The granular evidence of the mayoralty is consistent with everything else in his file: he kept the apartment in Harlem; he refused the security detail in its full form; he held court at street level; he insisted on visible presence in the boroughs rather than ceremonial appearances; he clashed predictably with the city's enforcement and finance apparatus. He also discovered, as the file would have predicted, that the office requires compromises that his code does not accommodate. The arc terminated with him leaving the role — the same loop as Thunderbolts, scaled up by an order of magnitude: accept on principle, hold as long as honorable, walk on principle.

Critically, this round of the loop cost more. The mayoralty is not a job one resigns cleanly. The file assesses the post-mayoral period as carrying a measurable residue of disillusionment that was not present at comparable previous exit points. Where the post-Thunderbolts Cage returned briskly to Heroes for Hire and resumed normal operations, the post-mayoral Cage has demonstrated a longer reset period and a more pronounced retreat into family-and-Harlem perimeter.

### 4.4 Marital Status: Jones, J. — Current

The marriage is the most stable load-bearing structure in the subject's life and remains intact in the present window. Granular indicators across recent canon:

- **Domicile.** They maintain residence in or adjacent to Harlem. The choice of neighborhood is non-negotiable on his side and accommodated on hers; the file reads this as one of the durable compromises that makes the marriage work — she gives him the geography, he gives her professional latitude.
- **Division of operational labor.** Jones runs Alias Investigations as an independent concern; the subject does not interfere with her cases and she does not interfere with his. They share intelligence informally and consult on cases that overlap. Childcare is shared, with extended-family supplementation (Misty Knight, the broader Heroes for Hire network, and on documented occasions Rand).
- **Conflict pattern.** Recorded fights tend to follow two scripts: (1) one of them has concealed risk-exposure from the other (his pattern more than hers, but hers also); (2) one of them has been operationally co-opted by an outside force (mind control, possession, framing) and the other has had to respond. The marriage has survived multiple instances of each. The mutual recovery pattern — verbal disclosure, sometimes prolonged silence, eventual physical reconciliation, no recorded sustained estrangement — indicates a working repair mechanism.
- **Sexual and affective register.** Frank, mutual, durable. Public-affection register restrained but present; private register documented as warm and physically demonstrative. No recorded extramarital activity from either party in the current era.
- **Tell:** when stressed about Jessica specifically, his hands. He holds objects more carefully than he needs to. The standing canonical gag of him crushing a coffee mug or doorframe when startled is not how he registers spousal anxiety; the opposite — exaggerated gentleness, the man with the strength of fifty being conspicuously careful — is.

### 4.5 Parenthood: Cage, D. — Current

Danielle is now of an age at which she registers her father as a public figure as well as a parent, which introduces a new and ongoing strain that the file flags as the most likely future psychological pressure point. The subject's parenting style, documented across the recent decade:

- **Physically present.** He carries her, walks her, is photographed and depicted at her school, her doctor's appointments, her routine errands. This is not performative; it is consistent across panels in which he has no reason to know he is being observed.
- **Verbally restrained but emotionally open.** He talks to her like a person, not a child. He explains things rather than commanding. He uses humor with her in the same register he uses with Rand and Jones — the family dialect.
- **Code-transmissive.** He is actively teaching her his operational code in age-appropriate fragments: don't lie to family; the neighborhood is yours and you are its; people have to earn what they want from you; being scared is information, not weakness.
- **Visibly anxious about her safety in a way he does not display about his own.** This is the single largest gap between his self-presentation and his somatic state. When she is in proximity to operational risk, his baseline posture changes: shoulders forward, weight distributed forward over the balls of his feet, hands free and visible, head tracking the perimeter rather than the conversation. Anyone trained to read close-protection body language would identify it within seconds.
- **The Burstein dread, transmitted.** The file infers that his deepest current fear, not articulated openly in canon but legible in his choices, is that whatever was done to him at the cellular level might be heritable, transmissible, or weaponizable against the child. His response to any external interest in Danielle's biology — and there has been external interest, given the family's profile — is sharper and faster than his response to threats against himself.

### 4.6 The Rand Relationship — Current

The friendship with Daniel Rand persists as the second-load-bearing relationship of his life and as the only male peer attachment he has ever sustained. Current-era status:

- The Power Man and Iron Fist reunion arc (Walker run) repaired and re-established the partnership on adult-and-mutual terms after years of intermittent contact. The two men are different people than the young heroes who originally partnered; the affection survived the difference.
- Rand is godfather-adjacent to Danielle — present at significant family occasions, trusted with the child, integrated into the household's outer ring.
- The interpersonal dynamic remains identifiable across decades: Cage as the grounded, skeptical, deadpan straight man; Rand as the earnest, mystical, periodically ridiculous foil; both fluent in the shared dialect of mutual mockery that signals long-term male intimacy in this subject's interpersonal grammar.
- Cage continues to function as Rand's most reliable reality-test on questions of race, class, and street-level reality; Rand continues to function as Cage's most reliable reality-test on questions of spiritual and cosmic-scale reality. They calibrate each other.

### 4.7 The Harlem Position — Current

Geographic anchoring remains absolute. The subject lives in Harlem, eats in Harlem, conducts business out of Harlem, and treats the neighborhood as both jurisdiction and church. Granular present-era indicators:

- He is known on the block. The standing canonical depictions — being greeted by name on the street, being asked for selfies by neighborhood teenagers, being deferred to by older residents who remember the Carl Lucas era — are consistent across all current writers.
- He maintains informal infrastructure: relationships with specific bodega owners, barbers, restaurateurs, pastors (the Pop's-barbershop archetype recurs across his canon and is operationally accurate as a depiction of his social network). These relationships function as both his domestic comfort layer and his street-intelligence layer.
- He has refused, repeatedly, to relocate. Wealth, status, and security considerations have all been offered as reasons to move; he has declined each time. Harlem is identity, not preference.
- His relationship to the neighborhood's gentrification and demographic change is canonically acknowledged and tense. He is, in the current era, one of the older Black men in his immediate residential radius; he registers this and it weighs on him.

### 4.8 Professional Status — Current

The subject's professional operations in the present window are best described as **post-institutional**. After cycling through every major institutional role available — Avengers leadership, Thunderbolts leadership, the mayoralty — he has returned to the operating mode that has always best fit his code: small-unit, fee-for-service, neighborhood-anchored protection work, augmented by ad-hoc team-ups when the scale demands it.

- **Heroes for Hire** in its current iteration functions as the organizational shell. Roster fluid; core constants Cage, Rand, Misty Knight, intermittent Colleen Wing.
- **Fee structure** preserved as principle. He still charges. The fee is still negotiable for clients who genuinely cannot pay. The principle is the charging itself — the assertion that his labor has value and is not owed.
- **Avengers reserve status.** He is available to the broader Avengers structure but does not seek it. When called, he comes. When not called, he does not call.
- **Public profile.** Higher than at any prior point in his career due to the mayoral exposure. He has not fully metabolized this — the subject who built his identity on refusing to be invisible has discovered that hyper-visibility brings its own erosions, and the file records a measurable post-mayoral retreat from media-facing surfaces.

### 4.9 Recent Behavioral and Somatic Micro-Patterns (Present Window)

Updating the longitudinal pattern file with current-era specifics:

- **Posture.** Baseline upright, weight balanced; in domestic settings noticeably looser than in any prior era — he sits back, leans, occupies furniture comfortably. In operational settings, the old forward-loaded protective stance is intact and possibly more pronounced post-mayoralty.
- **Hands.** Continued exaggerated control around the family. A reflex of slightly opening and closing the right hand when stressed has been depicted across recent writers and reads as a self-regulation tic.
- **Voice.** Lower register than in his early-career depictions, less performatively gruff than in the Cage Vol. 1 wilderness era, more conversational than at any prior period. The "Sweet Christmas" exclamation persists but is deployed less frequently and more knowingly — increasingly used with a self-aware register, a deliberate signature rather than reflexive utterance.
- **Wardrobe.** Settled into the modernized civilian uniform: dark t-shirt or henley, jeans, jacket as weather requires. The yellow-shirt-and-tiara silhouette has been retired to nostalgia callbacks; the current presentation is unmistakably grown-man, working-class-Black-uptown register. The chain symbol persists in vestigial form (belt, accessory) — the metabolized object remains worn but no longer foregrounded. He has nothing left to prove with it.
- **Eating.** Continues to eat soul food, continues to drink coffee, continues to be photographed at the same handful of Harlem establishments. Diet is one of the most stable observable variables in his entire file.
- **Sleep.** Inferred disturbed at moderate baseline; better than at any prior recorded period; degraded acutely in the immediate post-mayoral months. He sleeps better when Jessica is in the apartment than when she is on a case. He sleeps worse when Danielle is out of the apartment than when she is in it. This is unremarkable for any parent; in his case it is operationally readable in his daytime irritability variance.
- **Media consumption.** Reads the local press attentively. Watches sports. Consumes Black cultural and political media at sustained engagement levels — the file infers ongoing private intellectual engagement that he rarely externalizes in dialogue.
- **Phone behavior.** Carries a phone, uses it minimally, prefers in-person conversation, distrusts text as an evidentiary medium (an old prison-shaped instinct about written records). He will answer Jessica's calls and Danielle's calls and Rand's calls reliably; other calls go to voicemail with a documented multi-hour delay.

### 4.10 Current Threat Surface

Active and credible threats against the subject in the present window:

- **Residual enemies from the mayoralty.** Political and criminal actors who lost ground during his administration retain motive. The threat surface from this category is broader and less personal than his historical rogues' gallery and is in some ways more dangerous because it is institutional rather than individual.
- **Legacy adversaries.** Diamondback remains the prototype, returns periodically, and reactivates the foundational complex each time. Bushmaster lineage. Various Burstein-procedure imitators and inheritors.
- **Family-targeted threat.** Danielle's profile as the daughter of two enhanced parents and a known associate of the Avengers structure makes her a recurring kidnap-target archetype. The subject is aware of this and lives with it.
- **Medical-experimental threat.** Any actor seeking to reproduce, weaponize, or reverse-engineer the Burstein process treats him as primary specimen. This category of threat is the one that most reliably routes around all his defenses, because it triggers the original wound directly.

### 4.11 Current Psychological State — Synthesis

The subject in the present window presents as a man who has, against substantial counter-evidence, achieved a workable equilibrium. He is married, parenting, geographically anchored, professionally autonomous, peer-attached, and physically intact. He is also more tired than at any prior point in his recorded life, more reluctant to accept new institutional asks, more openly protective of his domestic perimeter, and more conscious of mortality both his own and his daughter's.

The cPTSD signature persists at managed sub-threshold levels. The defenses remain mature-cluster dominant. The code remains intact. The chosen-family architecture has held and is now multi-generational. The Harlem anchor has held. The Rand attachment has held. The Jones attachment has held and deepened.

The single largest unresolved current pressure is the integration of the mayoral experience into his self-concept. He held an institutional office. He performed it as well as a man with his code could perform it. He left it for the same reasons he leaves every institution. The file's current assessment is that he has not yet decided what this episode means about him, and that the next major arc of his psychological life will turn on what conclusion he eventually draws — whether the mayoralty proved that his code can inhabit institutional power without corruption (in which case future institutional asks become harder to refuse), or whether it proved that institutional power corrodes the code regardless of who holds it (in which case the post-institutional retreat becomes permanent).

The file's working prediction is the latter, on the basis of the entire prior pattern. The subject has spent fifty years demonstrating, with remarkable consistency, that he will accept any institutional role offered in good faith and walk away from any institutional role that compromises his code, and that the walking-away is the part that defines him. The mayoralty is unlikely to have reversed that. What it has done is raise the cost of the next acceptance, and the file flags this as the variable to watch across the next operational window.

**Current location:** Harlem.
**Current status:** Active, married, parenting, post-institutional, equilibrium maintained with elevated fatigue baseline.
**Current operational readiness:** High.
**Current willingness to be called:** Low and earned.

— end segment 04 —


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: CAGE, LUCAS (b. Carl Lucas)

*Compiled from corroborated canonical incident, clinical inference from observed presentation, and reconstructed somatic timeline. Where formal records do not exist (the subject has no continuous primary-care relationship across the file period), entries are derived from incident reportage and direct observation.*

---

## 1. Constitutional Baseline and Pre-Procedural Status

**Anthropometrics (post-procedure, stable across file period):** Height 6'6" (198 cm). Mass 425 lb (193 kg) at metahuman density — note that this figure is misleading on standard scales; the subject's tissue density is substantially elevated, so his volumetric profile reads as a large but not freakishly outsized man. Practitioners attempting to estimate his weight visually consistently underestimate by 80–120 lb, a fact that has had operational consequences (collapsed flooring, failed elevator weight calculations, one documented incident involving a hospital gurney).

**Pre-procedural baseline (Carl Lucas, ages 0–early 20s):** Unremarkable Black male, peak-athletic build cultivated through street-level conditioning rather than formal training. Boxing exposure in adolescence (Bloods-era social environment); some evidence of orthopedic micro-trauma typical of young men in unstructured combat — healed nasal fracture (pre-procedure, visible as a barely-perceptible deviation), scarring on the dorsum of both hands consistent with bare-knuckle fighting, a chipped right lateral incisor that was never restored and remains visible only when he laughs broadly. No chronic conditions on record. Childhood vaccinations presumed complete (Harlem public-school enrollment record implies). No allergies documented.

**Family medical history (relevant):** Father James Lucas — longevity unknown at this writing, cardiac risk profile typical for Black men of his cohort and generation (untreated hypertension probable, given era and socioeconomics; the deacon's diet of soul-food staples is the same diet the subject inherited). Mother — deceased early; cause of death not in the open record but the subject's reluctance to speak of her, combined with the era and the absence of any "long illness" narrative, suggests acute cause (cerebrovascular event, complication of childbirth in the case of a later pregnancy, or community-violence proximity — the file marks this as unresolved). Brother James Jr. ("Coldfire"/Stryker) — later subjected to his own metahuman exposure event; pre-existing constitution presumed similar. No documented hereditary disorders. The Lucas men are large, durable, and tend to die of things other than their bodies.

---

## 2. The Seagate Period — Pre-Procedural Trauma Inventory

Two-plus years incarcerated in Seagate Prison (Georgia). The medical history of this period is *not* clean and is the proximal substrate on which the Burstein procedure was performed.

**Documented and inferable injuries:**

- Repeated soft-tissue trauma from beatings administered by Officer Albert "Billy Bob" Rackham and subordinates. Pattern consistent with truncheon strikes to the back, ribs, and posterior thighs (locations chosen to avoid visible facial injury — standard carceral practice for hiding abuse). Several rib fractures probable, healed without setting. Persistent low-grade thoracic pain in the years immediately following is implied by the subject's posture in early Hero for Hire panels — a slight rightward guarding when seated, which disappears entirely after he settles into the post-procedural body.
- At least one closed-fist orbital contusion (left), healed without surgical intervention.
- Knuckle and metacarpal damage from yard fights — the subject defended himself successfully and frequently.
- Chronic sleep deprivation. Solitary confinement episodes (Rackham used isolation punitively). This is the origin of the subject's lifelong tendency toward shallow, vigilant sleep — discussed in §6.
- Nutritional inadequacy — Seagate-era weight likely 15–25 lb below his pre-incarceration baseline. Subject has spoken once, briefly, of "prison-thin" as a thing he remembers in his body.
- Probable dental neglect: no record of cleanings, fillings, or extractions during incarceration. The subject's adult dental presentation is good, which suggests private restorative work in the early Hero for Hire period that he has not discussed.

**Psychological residue specific to the medical/somatic dimension:** Carcerality is encoded in his body before any superhuman alteration. The hypervigilance he carries is not first a response to being shot at — it is a response to being touched without consent in confined space. This is operationally important. When restrained, examined, or even firmly handled by clinicians, his autonomic response is disproportionate to the stimulus. Field medics have noted that he will *allow* hands on him but does not *relax* under them; the pulse at his carotid (when palpable, see below) accelerates rather than slows during medical contact.

---

## 3. The Burstein Procedure — Index Event

**Date:** Final months of Seagate incarceration. **Administered by:** Dr. Noah Burstein. **Sabotaged by:** Officer Albert Rackham. **Subject's consent status:** Coerced — parole leverage was the consideration offered. This is not informed consent under any modern standard; the file should mark this as **medical assault under color of state authority.**

**Procedure as designed:** Cellular regeneration / metabolic acceleration immersion, derived from the Erskine/Reinstein super-soldier protocol lineage. Subject immersed in an electrostimulated chemical bath; intent was modest enhancement of healing rate and constitutional resilience. Designed dose: sub-threshold for full Class-superhuman conversion.

**Procedure as administered:** Rackham, intending homicide-by-equipment-malfunction, increased the bath's power output past safety tolerances. The intended sub-threshold dose became a supra-threshold one. The subject did not die; the procedure overshot.

**Acute outcome (presenting symptoms during and immediately post-procedure):**
- Generalized full-body pain described later as "every cell on fire at once."
- Visible alteration of skin tone and surface light-refraction — the dermis assumed its present near-impermeable character within minutes.
- Strength gain manifest immediately (the subject broke free of his restraints, then the chamber, then the cell block, then the prison wall).
- No documented loss of consciousness, but transient disorientation consistent with metabolic shock.

**Sustained physiological alterations (the steady-state, present across all subsequent eras):**

- **Integumentary:** Epidermis and dermis modified to ballistic-resistant density. Withstands conventional small-arms fire (.22 through .45 ACP without penetration), most knives, fragmentation, fire to ~2000°F for limited duration, and significant blunt-force impact. Vulnerabilities documented under §5.
- **Musculoskeletal:** Skeletal density increased substantially; muscle attachments reinforced; tendon and ligament tensile strength scaled to match. Lifting capacity in the Class-25-to-50 range depending on adrenaline state and writer-era. The strength is partially exertion-responsive — sustained effort against immovable resistance produces measurable temporary further increase, an unusual property suggesting the procedure left him with a residual adaptive metabolism.
- **Cardiovascular:** Heart muscle correspondingly densified. Resting heart rate exceptionally low (estimated 38–44 bpm). Blood pressure difficult to measure — sphygmomanometer cuffs do not reliably compress the brachial artery against the densified surrounding tissue. Carotid pulse palpable only to a trained hand applying pressure that would bruise a normal subject.
- **Pulmonary:** Increased breath-hold capacity (documented 8–12 minutes in field conditions). Lung tissue presumed densified but retains elasticity.
- **Metabolic:** Elevated baseline caloric requirement (estimated 6,000–8,000 kcal/day at activity; subject's documented preference for substantial meals reflects this). Slow but eventual processing of alcohol and most pharmaceuticals — see §7.
- **Neurological:** No documented cognitive impairment from the procedure; reflexes if anything sharpened. CNS sheathing presumed to share dermal-density properties, which is the primary reason concussive injury is rare even when the skull is impacted hard enough to crack masonry behind it.
- **Sensory:** Hearing, vision, olfaction within normal human ranges. He is not augmented in this dimension and has never claimed to be. Pain perception is preserved — this is critical and frequently misunderstood. He *feels* what hits him; he simply does not break.

**Psychological impact of the procedure itself (distinguished from impact of the powers):** This is the single most under-attended item in his medical file. The subject was experimented on, without meaningful consent, by an institutional medical apparatus, with the intent (on Rackham's part) of killing him. Every capacity he has been celebrated for since is the residue of a state-sponsored attempt on his life dressed in a lab coat. The proper comparison is Tuskegee. His subsequent lifelong refusal of medical care except under emergency conditions, his refusal to permit Stark or Reed or any third party to "study" his physiology even when offered as collaborative research, his immediate distrust of any institutional figure offering to "help" him chemically — all of this is rational. The needle-aversion noted in §7 is not phobia; it is memory.

---

## 4. The Body As Symbol — Self-Inscription on the Altered Form

A surveillance-grade medical file must note what the subject has done *to* his post-procedural body deliberately, as distinct from what was done to it.

- **No tattoos.** Notable. Most men of his demographic, generation, and incarceration history carry ink; he does not. Inference: the body was inscribed on by the state without his consent; he declines to inscribe further. The skin is a site of refusal.
- **No piercings.** Practical (his skin would resist the needle) and symbolic (same).
- **The chain belt (Hero for Hire era):** Worn directly against the skin at the waist. This is the only adornment he has carried for years at a time. The metabolic metaphor — wearing the imprisoning object as ornament — is discussed at length in §3 of the workup; medically, the relevant note is that the belt left no marks because nothing leaves marks.
- **Hair:** Has cycled through afro (Hero for Hire), close-cropped (Power Man/Iron Fist late period), and shaved (Cage Vol. 1 onward, predominant). The shaved head was adopted during a period of decompensation and has largely remained, with intermittent beard. The current presentation — shaved scalp, close beard — reads as low-maintenance, but is also tactically chosen: nothing for an opponent to grab.
- **Facial scarring:** Minimal. The pre-procedural chip on the right lateral incisor remains. A faint asymmetry at the left brow predates the procedure. Post-procedure, no new scars have accumulated despite documented exposures to incidents that should have left them — this is itself a documented finding.

---

## 5. Catalogue of Post-Procedural Injuries, Transformations, and Medical Events

Organized chronologically by era. Listed with mechanism, presentation, treatment, and somatic-psychological sequelae.

### 5a. Hero for Hire / Power Man Era (1972–1978)

- **Bushmaster encounter — multiple incidents.** Bushmaster is one of the few early antagonists whose enhanced strength approached Cage's pain threshold. Documented soft-tissue bruising (rare for the subject), one episode of cracked rib (right side, 7th–8th, healed without intervention in ~72 hours — an early indicator that his accelerated healing scales with the magnitude of the insult).
- **Chemistro's alchemy gun.** Localized transmutation attempts on the subject's arm and torso. The subject reports the sensation as "wrong, in the bone." No lasting alteration after the field was disrupted, but the episode established that his durability does not protect against reality-altering vectors — a vulnerability class he has been wary of since.
- **Piranha Jones — bite incident.** Jones's surgically-modified dentition failed against the subject's skin. Jones sustained dental fractures. The subject sustained a localized pressure bruise that resolved in hours. Operationally significant: he laughed afterward. This is the first recorded instance of the humor-as-defense pattern stabilizing in adult form.
- **Burstein and Temple kidnap / blackmail episode.** No personal injury but extreme physiological stress markers — sustained sympathetic activation over a multi-day arc. Subject reports headaches for the first time in his post-procedural life (likely tension-pattern, not vascular). Resolution restored baseline.
- **Cumulative across the era:** First sustained period in which the subject lived in his enhanced body without expecting it to be taken from him. The medical history of this era is mostly the absence of medical history — he stopped breaking. The psychological adjustment to no longer being injurable was nontrivial and is reflected in the slightly theatrical, almost performative physicality of his early-era body language: he is testing what he is.

### 5b. Power Man and Iron Fist Era (1978–1986)

- **Sustained low-level injury accumulation from team operations.** Most resolved without medical attention.
- **Adamantium-edged weapons exposure (rare, isolated).** The subject's skin can be cut by adamantium and by sufficiently exotic edges. Minor lacerations documented; healing within hours.
- **Toxin exposures (The Hand and analog actors).** The subject's impermeable skin paradoxically complicates ingested- and respiratory-route toxin treatment, because intravenous reversal cannot easily be administered. Documented in this era: at least one episode of respiratory-route exposure (gas-borne neurotoxin) requiring assisted ventilation administered through forced airway access — the field medic on record (Rand, with martial-arts-informed pressure-point technique) had to physically open and maintain the airway. The subject was conscious enough afterward to make a joke about it; he has not, on record, ever discussed how it felt to be unable to breathe and unable to be helped through ordinary means.
- **Rand "death" event and its somatic consequences.** No physical injury directly, but the post-event year shows clear somatization of grief: weight loss (estimated 20+ lb despite his metabolic floor), reported irritability and sleep disruption, increased reckless engagement (taking hits he didn't need to take). This is the first clearly visible episode of *grief expressed through the body rather than through speech.* The pattern repeats.

### 5c. Wilderness Years / Cage Vol. 1 (1992 era)

- **Combat injury rate elevated** — partly era-aesthetic, partly genuine decompensation behavior. The subject took unnecessary risks. Healing capacity absorbed the cost.
- **Several near-piercing events** from progressively exotic weapons developed specifically to defeat his skin. Each tested the upper limit of his durability and added to a cumulative file of "what works on him" that he has subsequently treated as classified information.
- **Possible alcohol use uptick** in this era — non-dependent, but a noticeable shift from his baseline near-abstinence. Resolved as the era ended.

### 5d. Modern Era — Alias / Pulse / New Avengers / Marriage (2001–2007)

- **Reintroduction of sexual intimacy on the record (Jones).** Medically: the subject is sexually functional; his density does not impair the act, though it imposes practical considerations (mass, force modulation) that the partnership has, by all accounts, accommodated.
- **Conception and fatherhood (Danielle).** Reproductive function intact; no documented genetic transmission concerns at the time of conception, though the daughter's later presentation has raised questions the subject has chosen not to pursue clinically.
- **Civil War combat exposures.** Sustained high-tempo engagement with SHRA enforcement units. Multiple bruising episodes, one electrostimulation weapon discharge of sufficient magnitude to drop him briefly (the only sustained loss of motor function in this era; recovered in <60 seconds). Psychological residue: confirmed that institutional force *can* reach him with the right tools, which has refined his threat-assessment but not his stance.
- **Skrull invasion episode (Secret Invasion era).** Sustained combat. No singular catastrophic injury but cumulative load.

### 5e. Cardiac Event / Depowering Arc (post–House of M era)

- **Acute cardiac episode** during a depowering sequence. The subject's heart, structurally adapted to function within densified surrounding tissue, was placed under acute stress when the densification temporarily reduced. Presentation consistent with myocardial strain rather than infarction; no permanent damage on subsequent imaging (when imaging has been possible).
- **Recovery:** Spontaneous, with restoration of powers. The subject has not voluntarily discussed the episode. He underwent no formal cardiac follow-up.
- **Psychological impact:** First clearly documented confrontation with his own mortality post-procedure. He had not, until this point, fully internalized that he could die of an ordinary cause. The subsequent year shows a marginal increase in protective behavior toward family — increased presence at home, reduced acceptance of distant missions — that did not previously characterize him. He never named the change; the behavior is the record.

### 5f. Civil War II Convalescence

- **Near-fatal injury** during the events of Civil War II. Specifics in the operational file. The relevant medical fact is that he was, for an extended period, *unconscious and in a hospital bed.* This is one of perhaps three or four times in his adult life that the subject has been a medical patient in any formal sense.
- **Extended convalescence** — multi-week. Visible weight loss, atrophy minor (his musculature is metabolically maintained even in dormancy, which is one of the procedure's quieter gifts). Discharge AMA likely; he has never finished a medical course of care he could leave under his own power.
- **Psychological impact:** Major. This is the convalescence period in which the depressive episode noted in §4 of the workup manifests most clearly. Anhedonia, withdrawal from Jessica and Danielle in the immediate aftermath (then over-correction toward protective hovering), irritability with team and with Rand specifically. The episode resolved without formal treatment over approximately six to nine months.

### 5g. Cage (2017) — Corrupted Burstein Process / Degenerative Episode

- **Mechanism:** Exposure to a hostile variant of the Burstein process administered weaponized by an adversary. The subject's enhanced physiology was destabilized at the cellular level; presentation included visible degradation of skin integrity, fatigue not previously possible for him, and what the field record describes as "his body forgetting how to be itself."
- **Course:** Subacute deterioration over weeks. Treatment required reverse-engineering of the original procedure under conditions that the subject — for the first time — *requested.* This is documented as a discrete behavioral shift: the man who has refused medical attention his entire post-procedural life *asked for help.*
- **Resolution:** Successful, with full restoration of baseline.
- **Psychological impact:** This is the single most significant medical event of his life after the original procedure. It produced the first explicit, articulated mortality anxiety on the record. The driver was fatherhood — the prospect of Danielle losing him before he was finished being her father. The episode generated the only documented instance of the subject discussing his medical history voluntarily with a clinician (Burstein himself, in a context that doubled as a settling of accounts decades old). The conversation is not reproduced in the open record but the subject's affect in the months following — fractionally softer, fractionally more willing to be seen as vulnerable by his wife — suggests that something was metabolized.

### 5h. Mayor of New York / Devil's Reign Period

- **Stress-related symptomatology.** Sustained institutional role produced the first documented chronic-tension presentation of his adult life: jaw clench (visible bruxism wear was not present pre-mayoralty and appeared during it), headache pattern, shortened sleep. Resolved on exit from office.
- **Combat exposures during the Devil's Reign engagement** were within his usual tolerance.

---

## 6. Sleep, Diet, Reproductive, and Lifestyle Medicine

**Sleep:** Lifelong shallow sleeper with brief deep-sleep windows. Bed posture: supine, hands at sides or one across abdomen, never face-down. Will not sleep with his back to a door. Wakes fully and immediately at unfamiliar sound — the post-Seagate vigilance pattern, neither extinguished nor pathological-by-his-lights. Marriage has improved this somewhat; he sleeps more deeply beside Jessica than alone, the only reliably documented attachment-mediated physiological change in his profile. Total sleep need: low (5–6 hours functional baseline), partly metabolic, partly habituated.

**Diet:** Soul-food anchored. Documented preferences include fried chicken, collards, cornbread, oxtails, grits, salmon croquettes, and — across every era — coffee, taken black, in volume. Caloric intake high. The subject cooks; this is under-noted. He is a competent home cook with a specific repertoire inherited from his father's household, and the act of cooking for Jessica and Danielle is one of his stabilizing rituals. He eats slowly when he is at peace and very quickly when he is not — a tell.

**Substance use:** Alcohol, light to moderate, social. Beer preference. Will accept whiskey in specific company (Rand, occasionally Jones). No documented intoxication of operational concern in over two decades of file. Tobacco: never on record. Cannabis: not on record. Harder substances: categorically absent. The heroin frame-up by Stryker has produced a lifelong, near-total aversion to anything in that class — he will not be in the same room with it without visible disquiet, and has declined pain management offered in the opioid family even under conditions where it was clinically indicated.

**Caffeine:** The one substance he uses heavily. Multiple cups daily. Metabolic clearance is rapid; effect on him is mild.

**Reproductive:** Functional. One biological child (Danielle Cage). No documented contraceptive practice in marriage. No documented fertility complications.

**Sexuality:** Heterosexual, monogamous within marriage, sexually frank with his wife in a way prior eras of his life did not document. The intimacy is a developmental achievement and should be read as such; for a man whose body has been a site of state intrusion, choosing to be touched at all is a position taken.

---

## 7. Pharmacology and Clinical-Access Profile

**Medication metabolism:** Slow for most agents; effective dose for clinical response is substantially higher than population norms. Subject has historically refused to be a research case for the establishment of these doses, so field administration is empirical.

**Vascular access:** *The defining clinical problem of his care.* Standard IV cannulation is impossible. Documented field-medic adaptations include: oral and nasogastric routes where feasible; intraosseous access attempted on at least one occasion via the femur, with difficulty (specialized drill required); and, in the one well-documented Hand-toxin episode, transmucosal administration. Any care plan for this subject must begin with the assumption that ordinary venous access is not available. Burstein


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: CAGE, LUCAS

*The body as it has been observed, longitudinally, across five decades of recorded behavior. Where the file infers, it infers from durable behavioral pattern. The subject is large, dark-skinned, and metahumanly dense; the body reads differently than its dimensions predict, and most observers misread it in characteristic ways the subject has learned to exploit.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTION & STANDING PRESENCE

**Anthropometrics.** 6'6" standing, ~425 lbs at metahuman tissue density. Shoulder breadth approximately 26 inches across the acromial line; chest circumference in the 58–60 range at rest. Neck thick (19+), trapezius mass continuous with deltoid mass such that the line from ear to shoulder is a single muscular slope rather than the notched silhouette of an ordinary heavily-built man. Hands are disproportionately large even for the frame — knuckles flattened from repeated impact against materials harder than human bone is meant to strike. Wrists do not taper in the usual way; the radius and ulna sit close-packed under thickened skin, giving the forearm a cylindrical rather than tapered profile.

**Density tell.** The most diagnostic standing feature is what physicists would call his *settle.* When he stops moving, he sinks half an inch into whatever he is standing on if it is compressible — floorboards, asphalt in heat, subway grating, the foam of a hotel mattress. Surveillance personnel tracking him by floor-vibration in apartment buildings have recorded the signature: a deliberate, measured footfall delivering 1.9–2.2× the impulse of an equivalently-sized non-enhanced man, followed by a long damped oscillation as the structure absorbs the load. He has learned, over decades, to walk light when he wishes — he can move silently on a wood floor — but the default is heavy and the heaviness is intentional. Heaviness is how the room knows he is in it.

**Skin.** Visibly indistinguishable from ordinary skin at conversational distance: same pigmentation, same pore pattern, same hair distribution, same scarring he had pre-Seagate. Under examination the differences emerge — it does not depress under fingertip pressure the way ordinary skin does; capillary refill is slower because the dermal microvasculature operates against a stiffer matrix; sweat beads sit on the surface longer before absorbing or evaporating. Old scars from before the procedure remain (a small one above the left eyebrow from a childhood fall, a hairline mark on the right forearm from a kitchen accident before he was twelve); no scar has been added to his body since the Burstein process completed. The body is, in this precise sense, a closed archive — everything written on it was written before the cage.

---

## 2. POSTURE, STANCE, & WEIGHT DISTRIBUTION

**Resting standing posture.** Feet roughly shoulder-width, weight slightly forward on the balls — a fighter's distribution rather than a parade rest — but the knees soft, not locked. The pelvis is neutral; he does not stand with the hyperextended lower-back posture common to heavily-muscled men compensating for chest mass. Shoulders ride back and down, not squared up. The chin is level. He does not loom even when he could; looming is a posture for people who need the room to know they are large, and he has been the largest object in every room he has entered since 1972.

**Hands at rest.** Default position is hands open at his sides, fingers slightly curled — not fisted. The closed fist when standing is a stress tell (see §10). When seated, hands rest on the thighs or laced loosely in the lap; he very rarely crosses his arms across his chest in conversation. Crossed arms appear specifically in two contexts: when listening to a pitch he does not believe, and when standing watch over someone he loves who has been hurt.

**The Harlem stance.** On his own block — observed at the bodega corner of 125th and Lenox, outside the rebuilt Gem Theater site, on the front steps of any residence he has held — the posture loosens into a hip-shot lean, weight on one leg, the other foot turned out forty-five degrees, one shoulder dropped. This is the body of a man who is home, and the geographic precision of where the posture turns on is one of the most reliable surveillance markers in the file. Cross 110th going south and the shoulders square again within two blocks.

**Sitting.** He does not sit in chairs. He sits *on* them. Most furniture cannot quite hold him without complaint; he has learned to distribute weight onto whatever load-bearing structure exists — the front edge of a couch's wood frame, the rail beneath a kitchen chair, the cinderblock under a porch step. In booths he angles diagonally so his weight passes through the bench's leg-bolt rather than its center. In folding chairs he is reluctant; in plastic chairs he refuses, politely, by leaning against a wall instead. This is not vanity. Furniture breaking under him reads to bystanders as a joke or a threat, neither of which he will perform on demand.

---

## 3. GAIT

**Walking.** Stride length approximately 34–36 inches, cadence ~95–100 per minute at relaxed pace — slow for a man his height, which conserves the impact signature and reads as unhurried. Heel-strike is deliberate; he does not roll through the foot the way an athlete-runner does, he plants. Arms swing modestly; the right arm slightly less than the left, an old protective bias from when he carried things in his right hand on a regular basis (likely Seagate-era, carrying meals and shop materials).

**Block-walk vs. street-walk.** On Harlem blocks his pace drops another 10–15%, head-on-a-swivel pattern engages (eyes sweep across stoops, doorways, second-floor windows — a continuous, low-amplitude scan that does NOT register as paranoia because he is also greeting people). Off his territory the pace increases slightly, the scan tightens to a narrower frontal cone, and the right hand drifts marginally closer to centerline — preparation for a strike that he has never, in surveillance memory, actually had to throw on a street.

**Stair behavior.** Takes stairs one at a time at normal pace; two at a time only when in a hurry; never three. He is conscious that crumbled stairs are a tell.

**Running.** Rare. He has the top speed of an enhanced sprinter but the gait of a man who finds running undignified. When pursuing he prefers to intercept by reading routes rather than chasing. When running he is heavy-footed in a way that is operationally loud — he can be tracked through a building by ear from two floors away.

**The bodega doorway pattern.** He turns slightly sideways through standard doorways without thinking about it. The angle is approximately 15 degrees off-square, just enough to clear shoulder width without making contact. He has done this for so long that he does it through doorways he could pass through straight; the body forgot when it was unnecessary.

---

## 4. HEAD, FACE, AND OCULAR PATTERNS

**Head carriage.** Held level. He does not tilt his head in conversation the way curious-listener archetypes do; the head stays still while the eyes do the work. When genuinely puzzled by a person, he tilts the chin DOWN rather than to the side — a subtle drop of one to two centimeters that brings the brow into the field and makes the next sentence land harder.

**Eyes.** Long blink interval at rest — measured at 4–6 seconds in calm conversation, dropping to 2–3 seconds under social demand. Gaze is direct and unhurried. He does not perform eye contact aggressively, but he does not break it first in conversations with authority figures. With intimates the gaze softens at the outer corners; with strangers it remains level and the outer corners stay flat. The scan pattern in unfamiliar rooms is consistent: door, then windows (clockwise), then occupants left-to-right, then the door again, all within four to six seconds of entry, all without obvious head movement. He sees the exits before he sees the people. He has done this since 1973.

**Eyebrows.** Heavy, mobile, expressive. The right eyebrow lifts independently — a learned tic, originally adopted as a substitute for the verbal skepticism his father punished him for. It now serves as his most efficient signal of disbelief, used most often when Stark-tier or institutional-tier interlocutors are explaining themselves.

**Mouth.** Default neutral with the corners slightly upturned — a base expression that reads as approachable to civilians and unreadable to predators. Smiles come in three distinct configurations: (a) the closed-mouth quarter-smile reserved for acquaintances and polite distance; (b) the full open smile, teeth visible, that he reserves almost exclusively for Danielle, for Jessica in private, for Rand on first sight after a separation, and for elderly Harlem residents who knew him as a child; (c) the wry asymmetric pull at the right corner, often accompanying "Sweet Christmas," that signals exasperated amusement. The full smile produces visible eye-crinkling and a brief head-tilt down-and-back; it is the most reliable index in the file of who is actually inside his trusted circle.

**Jaw.** Strong masseter development from years of clenching. The clench is a documented stress tell — the muscle visibly thickens at the angle of the mandible when he is suppressing speech, particularly during institutional encounters and particularly when the words *register* or *registration* are spoken near him. Bruxism is suspected but unconfirmed; he has never sought dental care for it.

**Vocal apparatus.** Voice is a low baritone, ~95–110 Hz at conversational pitch, dropping to 80–90 Hz under threat (he gets quieter and lower, not louder and higher; an inversion of the alarm pattern most subjects display). Resonance is chest-dominant. He articulates carefully — the diction is precise without being formal, and he code-switches register fluidly without changing the underlying vocal placement. He almost never raises his voice; recorded shouts in the file are sufficiently rare that each one is a dateable event.

---

## 5. SPEECH, LANGUAGE, & PARAVERBAL PATTERN

**Catchphrase function.** "Sweet Christmas" — used since the early Hero-for-Hire period, never replaced despite multiple opportunities to drop it. Surveillance analysis identifies three operational uses: (1) genuine surprise discharge, where it functions as the profanity-substitute it was originally designed to be; (2) tension-management in groups, where it cues bystanders that the moment is not yet violent; (3) recognition signal among intimates, where Jessica or Rand can prompt it from him as a check-in that he is still himself. The phrase has not appreciably weakened with use; he means it every time, in a way that is unusual for catchphrases of its vintage.

**Filler patterns.** Almost none. He does not say *um* or *uh*; instead he pauses, sometimes for two or three seconds, and the pause is the filler. The pauses do not register as searching for words — they register as deciding whether to spend them.

**Cursing.** Profanity is real and bilingual in register — he swears in standard English in private with adult intimates and almost never in front of children, civilians, or authority figures. The "Sweet Christmas" substitution was originally adopted, by his own implication, because his father would not abide profanity; it has outlived the father and become a chosen habit rather than an obedient one.

**Sentence shape.** Short declaratives under stress; longer, rhythmically Black-English-inflected periodic sentences when teaching, lecturing, or delivering a moral position. The Civil War–era speeches and the Thunderbolts-resignation register both deploy the longer form, which is his oratorical voice — closer to the deacon-father's pulpit cadence than the subject would acknowledge.

**Laugh.** A single quiet exhale through the nose for most amusement; a full diaphragmatic laugh, head back, mouth open, only with Rand or with Danielle and rarely with Jessica. The full laugh is loud enough to be heard through a closed apartment door and is recorded perhaps two dozen times in the entire surveillance period.

---

## 6. GROOMING, DRESS, AND SELF-PRESENTATION

**Hair.** Has cycled through three durable configurations: (a) the early-1970s modest afro of the original Hero-for-Hire period; (b) the shaved scalp of the Cage Vol. 1 wilderness years, which corresponded operationally with the angriest period of his life; (c) the close-cropped fade and trimmed beard of the modern era. Transitions between configurations are reliable mood markers — the shaved head returns under depressive or acting-out conditions; the closer the crop, the further from baseline. Cuts are received at a Harlem barbershop on a roughly three-week cycle, same chair, same barber for years at a stretch, conversation low, tip generous.

**Facial hair.** Maintained at approximately 1/4-inch length in the modern era, edge sharp, mustache continuous with the beard. He shaves the neckline himself with a straight razor — the only blade in the apartment that requires sharpening, kept on a leather strop above the bathroom sink. The skin will not take a razor cut, but the hair cuts normally, which means he is one of the few people on earth who can shave at full speed without risk. He does so quickly, never looking at the mirror longer than function requires.

**Clothing.** Across all eras, three constants: (1) clothing is sized large for an enhanced frame and replaced often because seam-stress destroys garments faster than wear-stress; (2) preference for solid colors, dark palette, with one chromatic anchor (the original yellow shirt; later, a yellow t-shirt under outerwear; in low-affect periods, the yellow disappears entirely); (3) the chain-belt or its substitutes — there is almost always one piece of broken-or-modified restraint hardware on his person, sometimes as a literal belt, sometimes as a necklace under the shirt, sometimes (in the recent period) as a bracelet pulled to inside-the-cuff invisibility. This is the durable somatic signature most outsiders miss: he wears the cage somewhere on his body every day.

**Tiara/headband.** Long retired. Its absence is its own datum; he has not worn ornamental gold above the eyes since the late 1970s and there is no indication he will again. The body has stopped costuming as a body and started costuming as a man.

**Smell.** Soap (unscented or lightly bay-rum), cocoa-butter lotion on the elbows and the back of the neck, and the faint mineral smell that enhanced-tissue subjects sometimes acquire from prolonged metabolic acceleration. He does not wear cologne. He sweats less than an unenhanced man at equivalent exertion and the sweat is nearly odorless.

---

## 7. EATING, DRINKING, AND METABOLIC HABIT

**Caloric load.** Estimated 6,500–8,500 kcal/day at maintenance, climbing past 12,000 during active combat periods. Documented preference for soul food — fried chicken, collards, mac and cheese, cornbread, oxtails, red beans and rice — sourced from a small rotation of Harlem establishments and from his own kitchen, where he cooks competently if not adventurously. Sundays after church-adjacent hours have, since childhood, been the heaviest eating day, a residual rhythm from the deacon-father's household.

**Eating posture.** Forks held in the right hand, American-style; elbows off the table (a paternal rule that survived the father). He eats with the slowest pace of any person at any given table — partly because of jaw mechanics against the density of his own facial muscles, partly because the food does not run out and there is no Seagate-era hurry to defend it, though he had to teach himself out of the Seagate-era hurry deliberately. Surveillance from the early post-prison years shows the prison pace; modern footage shows the corrected pace. The correction is one of the cleanest examples in the file of a body retrained against its trauma.

**Coffee.** Black, two cups at breakfast, occasional third in the afternoon. He prefers diner coffee to specialty coffee and has been overheard refusing the latter politely on multiple occasions. The cup is held in the right hand, by the body not the handle — his fingers fit poorly through standard mug handles, and the cup does not burn him.

**Alcohol.** One or two beers at social occasions; rarely spirits; never to intoxication in any recorded incident. He does not get drunk because he metabolizes alcohol too quickly for accumulation, and he is aware of this; the drinking is social-symbolic rather than affective.

**Water.** Drinks ordinary amounts. Does not carry a water bottle.

**Absences.** No tobacco. No cannabis (post-Reva). No harder substances, ever. The abstinence from heroin in particular is total and has the affective texture of a vow rather than a preference.

---

## 8. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Bedding.** A reinforced platform bed in the Harlem residence — the original frame was rebuilt with steel angle-iron at the corners and a 1-inch plywood understructure to keep the mattress from compressing through standard slats. Mattress is firm, replaced annually because of cumulative deformation under his density.

**Posture.** Sleeps on his back, arms at his sides or one across the chest. Does not snore (airway tissues are too dense to vibrate at sleep-airflow rates). Breath rate at sleep is slow, 8–10/min, and the chest rise is shallow but visible across the room.

**Onset and architecture.** Sleep onset is fast (3–7 minutes) when the household is intact and the door is locked from the inside; slow (30+ minutes) when separated from Jessica or Danielle, or when bunking off-residence. REM is intact; dream activity is rarely reported aloud, but eyelid-twitch and small finger movements are observable in the later cycles. Total sleep is short — 5 to 6 hours nightly is typical; he requires less than a baseline human of his mass and has done so since the Burstein procedure.

**Waking.** Wakes once between 0300 and 0400 most nights, sits up, listens to the apartment for 30–90 seconds, and lies back down. This is invariant across eras and is the single most reliable nocturnal marker in the file. The check is Seagate residue and is not interpreted as pathological; it is a household-watch behavior that has become a household-watch ritual. On Avengers premises he extends the check to a full walk through common areas.

**Dreams / disturbance.** Documented through partner report only. Jessica has indicated, obliquely, two recurring disturbance contents: prison-cell containment and the inability to reach someone calling his name. He does not initiate discussion of either. He sweats through sheets only after combat operations involving children harmed.

---

## 9. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE PATTERNS

**Frame.** Monogamous within marriage. Sexually frank as a verbal matter — willing to discuss it in adult company without prudery — but operationally private; the marriage's sexual life is conducted entirely within the residence, never advertised, never used as performance.

**Touch behavior with intimates.** A wide repertoire of low-pressure contact: hand to the small of the back when guiding Jessica through a doorway, palm flat between Danielle's shoulder blades when carrying her, forearm-to-forearm clasp on greeting Rand. The hand-to-back gesture with Jessica is the most consistent affectional micro-gesture in the file and persists across decades; it functions as a continuous re-verification of presence. With Danielle he is one-armed often — child on the hip, opposite hand free — and the carrying side alternates, an unconscious load-balance that suggests he has thought about not favoring one arm over a parenting lifetime.

**Force calibration in intimacy.** A constant low-grade attentional task. He has had to learn pressure control with a body that can crush ordinary tissue, and the learning shows: handshakes are deliberate to the point of being slightly slow; he pulls Jessica toward him rather than gripping; he picks Danielle up by sliding hands under her rather than closing fingers around her ribs. None of this is anxious; all of it is automatic. The same force-calibration is visible when he handles fragile objects (coffee mugs, paperback books, his daughter's hair), and the consistency of the calibration across decades is one of the gentler facts in the file about him.

**Sexual affect.** Where elsewhere his face is composed, sexual contexts produce visible softening of the eye-corners, the full smile (see §4), and a deeper, slower voice than baseline. Recovery to public composure after intimacy is rapid — under five minutes — and complete; there is no afterglow visible to an outside observer.

---

## 10. STRESS, THREAT, AND DECOMPENSATION TELLS

**Stage 0 — baseline.** All of the above defaults.

**Stage 1 — operational pressure.** Jokes drop out first; the quarter-smile flattens; sentences shorten; the right eyebrow stops moving. Breathing slows. He becomes more still rather than more active, which is a misleading signal to inexperienced observers — the calmer he looks on the surface, the closer he is to acting.

**Stage 2 — threat to chosen unit.** The fist closes at the side, knuckles pale. The chin drops 1–2 cm. The voice drops a full register, often to a near-whisper. The forward weight on the balls of the feet increases; the rear heel may come off the ground in fractional millimeters. He stops blinking for periods of 10+ seconds. Skin temperature at the back of the neck rises measurably. He has been observed to crack the surface of whatever he is touching — countertop, doorframe, the arm of a chair — without appearing to know he is doing it, and this is the cleanest physical-tell threshold in the file: when stone or wood under his fingertips begins to powder, the situation is one decision from violent.

**Stage 3 — betrayal/frame-up pattern reactivation.** Becomes verbose rather than quiet. This is the inversion that distinguishes Stage 3 from Stage 2 — when the trigger is the Stryker/Seagate pattern (being framed, being lied to by an ally, being told to comply), the body holds *still* and the mouth opens. He gives speeches in Stage 3. The eyes go cold and the diction sharpens; the cadence acquires the deacon-father's periodic structure; the right hand often comes up open-palmed in a teaching gesture. This is when institutions lose him.

**Stage 4 — decompensation under catastrophic loss.** Withdrawal from the chosen-family residence; geographic motion (often southbound or out of state); the head gets shaved; the yellow disappears from the wardrobe; the chain comes off the body and into a pocket. Sleep onset extends past 30 minutes. The waking-check at 0300 becomes a getting-up-and-walking event. Eating drops to one meal a day and shifts away from soul food toward whatever is fast and undignified. Speech to strangers drops to monosyllables. He fights more, talks less, smiles in none of the three configurations. Recovery is mediated almost entirely by re-entry into the chosen-family unit — Jessica or Rand or both appearing in person, persistently, until he comes home.

---

## 11. COMBAT KINESIOLOGY

**Stance.** Squared, slightly low, hands open and at sternum height; not a boxer's guard, because his face does not need protection. The open hand is the operational signature — he prefers grabs, shoves, and palm-strikes to closed-fist punches, because closed-fist punches at his force level often kill, and the no-kill rule is somatically enforced at the level of the h


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — SUBJECT: CAGE, LUCAS

---

## 1. ATTACHMENT STYLE: ORIGINS AND CURRENT ORGANIZATION

### 1.1 The Family-of-Origin Template

The subject's attachment architecture is built on a particular kind of childhood double-bind that the developmental literature labels **disorganized**: the same figures who provided care also provided harm, and the child had no coherent strategy available to resolve which face the caregiver would present. James Lucas Sr. — the deacon, the father — was the household's moral instrument: he taught right and wrong, modeled rectitude, and was emotionally legible only in the register of judgment. He did not hit at random; he hit on principle. This is, paradoxically, harder to integrate than randomness, because the principle implicates the child in his own punishment. The child learns: *to be loved by this man, I must be good; to be good is not enough; when I am bad I am cast out; when I am cast out I am also still being watched.*

The mother's early death removed the only counterweight. The record gives her almost no texture, which is itself diagnostic — she is a structural absence in the subject's narrative, the not-present third point that would have made the father's verdicts negotiable. Her loss is a wound he does not narrate. He rarely speaks her name in canon. The silence is consistent with grief that was never permitted formal expression in the household — a deacon's house does not have room for a son's long mourning.

Then James Jr. The brother dynamic is the keystone of the subject's relational template, and every subsequent betrayal in his life is filtered through it. The framing-for-theft episode is not a single incident; it is a developmental ontology. James Jr. takes the thing, Carl takes the blame, the father punishes Carl, James Jr. watches. Carl does not tell. The reasons he does not tell are themselves the wound: he loves his brother more than he trusts his father; he believes his father will not believe him; he has already learned that loyalty is paid for by the loyal one alone. He absorbs the cost. **This is the prototype: love costs more than it pays, and the bill comes to me.**

The disorganized substrate this produces is not the chaotic kind that decompensates into borderline organization in adulthood. It is the colder kind that consolidates into a working avoidant style with a permanent underground river of longing — the kind of attachment pattern that looks self-sufficient on the surface and is actually engaged in continuous, costly suppression of the wish to be held without being betrayed for it.

### 1.2 Adolescent Reinforcement

The Bloods era and the Stryker friendship are the second pass of the same lesson, this time with a peer instead of a sibling. Willis Stryker occupied, structurally, the older-brother slot James Jr. had vacated by failing it. The subject offered Stryker the loyalty that had cost him his father — and Stryker, when he believed he had been crossed, replied with the heroin-frame: the literal reproduction of the childhood scene, scaled to adult consequence. Carl Lucas was punished for protecting Reva from Stryker's lifestyle in exactly the way Carl Lucas had been punished for protecting his brother from their father. The fact that the punishment escalated from a beating in the kitchen to Seagate Prison did not change the shape; it confirmed it.

By the time the Burstein procedure overshoots and Luke Cage walks out of Seagate, the attachment template is set in its mature operational form: **trust is given slowly, given hard, and historically gets the giver hurt.** The wonder of the subsequent fifty years of life history is not that this template predicts his early behavior — it does — but that he has spent five decades deliberately, painfully refusing to let it predict him forever.

### 1.3 Current Style: Earned Secure With Disorganized Substrate

The shared workup's classification holds and is worth elaborating. Adult Cage presents, across the Bendis-and-after material, as functionally secure in his primary attachments: the Jessica Jones marriage is durable, sexually frank, conflict-tolerant, and reparative after rupture; the Rand partnership is the longest sustained peer bond in his canon and survives Rand's apparent death, Cage's framing for it, the years apart, and the resumption; the Claire Temple relationship in the early period ends without weaponized acrimony, which is itself a marker of earned security. He can tolerate being seen, being needed, being argued with, and being wrong without rupturing the bond.

But the substrate shows in specific places. He still flinches at certain offers of care — the medical-help kind specifically. He still goes physically distant when emotionally pierced rather than verbally close. He still requires the people closest to him to make the first move past the perimeter — Jones effectively kicked through his door across the Alias arc; Rand walked in over months of forced proximity; Temple was already inside the operational footprint before either of them admitted they were dating. He does not initiate intimate disclosure. He receives it, returns it, builds on it — but he does not start it.

This is what earned-secure-on-disorganized-substrate looks like in practice: the surface is competent and warm; the floor underneath is still tilted toward the door.

---

## 2. HOW HE BONDS

### 2.1 The Sequence

Bonding, for this subject, proceeds in an observable and remarkably consistent order across every significant attachment in the record. The stages:

1. **Proximity tolerance.** He simply allows the other person to be near him during operational time — at the office, on a case, on a team, in the building. He does not pursue; he does not refuse. This phase can last weeks (Temple, working in the same medical practice) to months (Rand, partnered on case after case) to years (Jones, in and out of his bed in the Alias period before either of them said the word "together").

2. **Operational reliance.** He lets the other person hold something that matters to a case. Hand him the bandage, drive the car, take the second floor, run the office while he's out. This is the first concrete trust. He notices, very carefully and without comment, whether the thing he handed over comes back the way he handed it over.

3. **Banter.** When he starts deploying humor at someone — "Sweet Christmas," the deadpan one-liners, the call-and-response with Rand — he is bonding. The humor is the connection-bid. People he does not joke with are people he does not yet trust.

4. **Domestic exposure.** He lets them into his actual living space. This is significant because the living space is also the operational hardpoint — his apartment, then his and Jones's home, are deliberately defensible and deliberately personal. Crossing the threshold is crossing the perimeter.

5. **Disclosure under prompt.** Eventually, when asked the right question by someone who has passed the previous stages, he will say something true about Seagate, about his father, about Reva, about the brother. He will not volunteer. He will answer, in short declarative sentences, and then change the subject. The disclosure is real. The discussion is not extended.

6. **Defense.** The final stage of bonding, for him, is when he begins to defend the other person *to himself* — when he catches himself organizing his actions around their well-being without having decided to. This is when, in his own internal accounting, the person has become his.

### 2.2 The Tells

Granular markers of where someone stands with him at any given moment:

- **Eye contact**: increases with trust. Strangers and authority figures get the long, level, neutral look — eye contact as evaluation, not connection. Trusted intimates get softer, more frequently broken eye contact — the eyes wander to their hands, their mouth, the room — because their presence does not require continuous threat-assessment.
- **Physical orientation**: he stands square-on to people he does not trust (he is presenting his harder front, ready to absorb) and slightly oblique to people he does (presenting a shoulder, relaxed posture).
- **Use of name**: he uses formal address ("Mr. Stark," "Director") as distance-keeping; uses first names with peers; uses nicknames (Danny, Jess, Doc) with intimates. The shift from "Iron Fist" to "Danny" in any given conversation is a barometer of the conversation's emotional temperature.
- **Voice register**: drops in pitch and slows in tempo with intimates; sharpens and shortens with adversaries. Under stress with intimates specifically, the voice gets quieter, not louder — which is the inverse of his stranger-stress behavior, and a useful tell.
- **Touch**: low baseline. With Jones, frequent and unselfconscious — hand on the back of her neck, palm flat on her sternum, the kind of contact that registers as ownership-of-the-relationship rather than possession-of-the-person. With Danielle, near-constant and visibly soothing for him as much as for her. With Rand, the contact is masculine-coded and brief — clasped forearm, shoulder strike, the hand-on-the-back-of-the-head pull-in. With nearly everyone else, including teammates, he does not initiate physical contact.

### 2.3 The Pace

He bonds *slowly* and *deeply*. The list of people he has actually bonded with, across fifty years of story, is short: Reva Connors (lost), Claire Temple (durable but eventually peripheral), Danny Rand (peer-primary), Jessica Jones (partner-primary), Danielle Cage (child-primary), Misty Knight (peer-secondary, via Rand), a small number of teammates who graduated from operational reliance to genuine trust (Cap qualifies in part; Spider-Man qualifies; most others do not). Compared to the sheer volume of acquaintances, allies, clients, and teammates he has interacted with, the actual bonded set is conspicuously small. He is not a collector. He is a curator.

---

## 3. HOW HE DISTRUSTS

### 3.1 The Default Setting

The baseline assumption, applied to all new actors, is that they are probably lying, probably extracting something, and probably backed by an institution that is also lying. This is not paranoia — paranoia requires non-reality-congruent suspicion, and his suspicion is exquisitely reality-congruent. It is **earned epistemic caution**, set as a default and adjusted downward only by evidence.

The settings differ sharply by category of person:

- **Institutional actors** (government, corporate, law enforcement, federal capes-and-suits): presumed compromised until proven personally trustworthy. The institution is never trusted; the individual within it may be, slowly. He distinguishes Steve Rogers the man from the SHRA the policy; he distinguishes Maria Hill the operator from SHIELD the apparatus.
- **Wealth**: distrust intensifies with wealth and decreases with proximity to manual work or to the neighborhood. He trusts Rand, who is wealthy, because Rand earned his bond before the wealth was salient and because Rand wears the wealth lightly. He does not trust most other billionaires he has worked with; the wariness is constant in the room with Stark.
- **Helpers**: people who offer to help him without being asked are evaluated with elevated suspicion. Charity is suspect. The offer reads as either pity (which insults him) or as the opening move of an extraction (which has historical precedent).
- **Strangers from Harlem**: the trust threshold is meaningfully lower. The geography itself is a credential.
- **Children**: trust is essentially default-on. He is markedly gentler with children than with adults, and the gentleness is one of the few places his guard simply is not up.

### 3.2 The Markers of Active Distrust

When he is actively distrusting someone in real time, the behaviors are specific:

- The previously-mentioned square-on body orientation.
- Hands visible, often at his sides, never in pockets — readiness without display.
- Conversational economy: yes, no, short sentences, no banter, no warmth in the voice.
- Quiet repetition of the other party's words back to them as a check — "You want me to do *what.*" The flat affect on the rephrasing is the tell.
